统计模型表中每条字符串长度小于14的模型路径在最近36小时内在根原因推断表的最优路径中出现的次数。	select count ( * ) from t_model_data left join t_inference_data on t_model_data.Inference_path = t_inference_data.Inference_path where length ( t_model_data.Inference_path ) < 14 and t_inference_data.Inference_time > addtime ( now ( ) , ' - 36 : 0 ' ) group by t_model_data.Inference_path ;
统计模型表中每条字符串长度小于15的模型路径在最近30小时内在根原因推断表的最优路径中出现的次数。	select count ( * ) from t_model_data left join t_inference_data on t_model_data.Inference_path = t_inference_data.Inference_path where length ( t_model_data.Inference_path ) < 15 and t_inference_data.Inference_time > addtime ( now ( ) , ' - 30 : 0 ' ) group by t_model_data.Inference_path ;
统计模型表中每条字符串长度小于1的模型路径在最近12小时内在根原因推断表的最优路径中出现的次数。	select count ( * ) from t_model_data left join t_inference_data on t_model_data.Inference_path = t_inference_data.Inference_path where length ( t_model_data.Inference_path ) < 1 and t_inference_data.Inference_time > addtime ( now ( ) , ' - 12 : 0 ' ) group by t_model_data.Inference_path ;
统计模型表中每条字符串长度小于19的模型路径在最近7小时内在根原因推断表的最优路径中出现的次数。	select count ( * ) from t_model_data left join t_inference_data on t_model_data.Inference_path = t_inference_data.Inference_path where length ( t_model_data.Inference_path ) < 19 and t_inference_data.Inference_time > addtime ( now ( ) , ' - 7 : 0 ' ) group by t_model_data.Inference_path ;
